It's assigned to one of the executors for processing.\n * 2. It's locked for committing, removal, other manipulations etc.\n * 3. Neither 1 or 2, i.e. it stays idle. This is possible if we do not have enough executors or because those tasks\n *    are not processable (e.g. because no records fetched) yet.\n */\npublic final class DefaultTaskManager implements TaskManager {\n\n    private final Time time;\n    private final Logger log;\n    private final TasksRegistry tasks;\n\n    private final Lock tasksLock = new ReentrantLock();\n    private final Condition tasksCondition = tasksLock.newCondition();\n    private final List<TaskId> lockedTasks = new ArrayList<>();\n    private final Map<TaskId, StreamsException> uncaughtExceptions = new HashMap<>();\n    private final Map<TaskId, TaskExecutor> assignedTasks = new HashMap<>();\n    private final TaskExecutionMetadata taskExecutionMetadata;\n\n    private final List<TaskExecutor> taskExecutors;\n\n    public static class DefaultTaskExecutorCreator implements TaskExecutorCreator {\n        @Override\n        public TaskExecutor create(final TaskManager taskManager, final String name, final Time time, final TaskExecutionMetadata taskExecutionMetadata) {\n            return new DefaultTaskExecutor(taskManager, name, time, taskExecutionMetadata);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public DefaultTaskManager(final Time time,\n                              final String clientId,\n                              final TasksRegistry tasks,\n                              final TaskExecutorCreator executorCreator,\n                              final TaskExecutionMetadata taskExecutionMetadata,\n                              final int numExecutors\n                              ) {\n        final String logPrefix = String.format(\"%s \", clientId);\n        final LogContext logContext = new LogContext(logPrefix);\n        this.log = ArrayList<>(numExecutors);\n        for (int i = 1; i <= numExecutors; i++) {\n            final String name = clientId + \"-TaskExecutor-\" + i;\n            this.taskExecutors.add(executorCreator.create(this, name, time, taskExecutionMetadata));\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public StreamTask assignNextTask(final TaskExecutor executor) {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            if (!taskExecutors.contains(executor)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The requested executor for getting next task to assign is unrecognized\");\n            }\n\n            // the most naive scheduling algorithm for now: give the next unlocked, unassigned, and  processable task\n            for (final StreamTask task : tasks.activeInitializedTasks()) {\n                if (!assignedTasks.containsKey(task.id()) &&\n                    !lockedTasks.contains(task.id()) &&\n                    canProgress(task, time.milliseconds()) &&\n                    !hasUncaughtException(task.id())\n                ) {\n\n                    assignedTasks.put(task.id(), executor);\n\n for executor {}\", executor.name());\n\n            return null;\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void awaitProcessableTasks(final Supplier<Boolean> isShuttingDown) throws InterruptedException {\n        final boolean interrupted = returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            for (final StreamTask task : tasks.activeInitializedTasks()) {\n                if (!assignedTasks.containsKey(task.id()) &&\n                    !lockedTasks.contains(task.id()) &&\n                    canProgress(task, time.milliseconds()) &&\n                    !hasUncaughtException(task.id())\n                ) {\n                    log.debug(\"Await unblocked: returning early from await since a processable task {} was found\", task.id());\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n            try {\n                // We re-check the shutdownRequest atomic boolean to avoid a race condition. If this thread was\n                // previously interrupted while awaiting tasksCondition, it is possible to miss the signalAll that\n                // is called during shutdown. If this happens, we end up blocking in the await forever.\n                if (!isShuttingDown.get()) {\n                    log.debug(\"Await blocking\");\n                    tasksCondition.await();\n                } else {\n                    log.debug(\"Not awaiting since shutdown was requested\");\n                }\n            } catch (final InterruptedException ignored) {\n                // we interrupt the thread for shut down and pause.\n                // we can ignore this exception.\n                log.debug(\"Await unblocked: Interrupted while waiting for processable tasks\");\n                return true;\n            }\n            log.debug(\"Await unblocked: Woken up to check for processable tasks\");\n            return false;\n        });\n\n        if (interrupted) {\n            throw new InterruptedException();\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void signalTaskExecutors() {\n        log.debug(\"Waking up task executors\");\n        executeWithTasksLocked(tasksCondition::signalAll);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void unassignTask(final StreamTask task, final TaskExecutor executor) {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            if (!taskExecutors.contains(executor)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The requested executor for unassign task is unrecognized\");\n            }\n\n            final TaskExecutor lockedExecutor = assignedTasks.get(task.id());\n            if (lockedExecutor == null || lockedExecutor != executor) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Task \" + task.id() + \" is not locked by the executor\");\n            }\n\n            assignedTasks.remove(task.id());\n\n            log.debug(\"Unassigned {} from executor {}\", task.id(), executor.name());\n            tasksCondition.signalAll();\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public KafkaFuture<Void> lockTasks(final Set<TaskId> taskIds) {\n        final KafkaFutureImpl<Void> result = new KafkaFutureImpl<>();\n\n        if (taskIds.isEmpty()) {\n            result.complete(null);\n            return result;\n        }\n\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            lockedTasks.addAll(taskIds);\n\n            final Set<TaskId> remainingTaskIds = new ConcurrentSkipListSet<>(taskIds);\n\n            for (final TaskId taskId : taskIds) {\n                final Task task = tasks.initializedTask(taskId);\n\n                if (task == null) {\n                    throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Trying to lock task \" + taskId + \" but it's not owned\");\n                }\n\n                if (!task.isActive()) {\n                    throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The locking task \" + taskId + \"    log.debug(\"Requesting release of task {} from {}\", taskId, executor.name());\n                    final KafkaFuture<StreamTask> future = executor.unassign();\n                    future.whenComplete((streamTask, throwable) -> {\n                        if (throwable != null) {\n                            result.completeExceptionally(throwable);\n                        } else {\n                            assert !assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId);\n                            // It can happen that the executor handed back the task before we asked it to\n                            // in which case `streamTask` will be null here.\n                            assert streamTask == null || streamTask.id() == taskId;\n                            remainingTaskIds.remove(taskId);\n                            if (remainingTaskIds.isEmpty()) {\n                                result.complete(null);\n                            }\n                        }\n                    });\n                } else {\n                    remainingTaskIds.remove(taskId);\n                    if (remainingTaskIds.isEmpty()) {\n                        result.complete(null);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            return result;\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public KafkaFuture<Void> lockAllTasks() {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() ->\n            lockTasks(tasks.activeInitializedTasks().stream().map(Task::id).collect(Collectors.toSet()))\n        );\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void         log.debug(\"Waking up task executors\");\n            tasksCondition.signalAll();\n        });\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void unlockAllTasks() {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> unlockTasks(tasks.activeInitializedTasks().stream().map(Task::id).collect(Collectors.toSet())));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void add(final Set<StreamTask> tasksToAdd) {\n executors\");\n            tasksCondition.signalAll();\n        });\n\n        log.info(\"Added tasks {} to the task manager to process\", tasksToAdd);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void remove(final TaskId taskId) {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            if (assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The task to remove is still assigned to executors\");\n            }\n\n            if (!lockedTasks.contains(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The task to remove is not locked yet by the task manager\");\n            }\n\n            if (!tasks.containsInitialized(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The task to remove is not owned by the task manager\");\n            }\n\n            tasks.removeTask(tasks.initializedTask(taskId));\n        });\n\n        log.info(\"Removed task {} from the task manager\", taskId);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Set<ReadOnlyTask> getTasks() {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> tasks.activeInitializedTasks().stream().map(ReadOnlyTask::new).collect(Collectors.toSet()));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setUncaughtException(final StreamsException exception, final TaskId taskId) {\n        executeWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n\n            if (!assignedTasks.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"An uncaught exception can only be set as long as the task is still assigned\");\n            }\n\n            if (uncaughtExceptions.containsKey(taskId)) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"The uncaught exception must be cleared before restarting processing\");\n            }\n\n            uncaughtExceptions.put(taskId, exception);\n        });\n\n        log.info(\"Set an uncaught exception of type {} for task {}, with error message: {}\",\n            exception.getClass().getName(),\n            taskId,\n            exception.getMessage());\n    }\n\n    public Map<TaskId, RuntimeException> drainUncaughtExceptions() {\n        final Map<TaskId, RuntimeException> returnValue = returnWithTasksLocked(() -> {\n            final Map<TaskId, RuntimeException> result = new HashMap<>(uncaughtExceptions);\n            uncaughtExceptions.clear();\n            return result;\n        });\n\n        if (!returnValue.isEmpty()) {\n            log.debug(\"Drained {} uncaught exceptions\", returnValue.size());\n        }\n\n        return returnValue;\n    }\n\n    public boolean hasUncaughtException(final TaskId taskId) {\n        return returnWithTasksLocked(() -> uncaughtExceptions.containsKey(taskId));\n    }\n\n    private void executeWithTasksLocked(final Runnable final StreamTask unassignedTask = unassignCurrentTask();\n                    taskReleaseFuture.complete(unassignedTask);\n                } else {\n                    log.debug(\"Asked to return current task, but returned current task already.\");\n                    taskReleaseFuture.complete(null);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        private void handleException(final StreamsException e) {\n            if (currentTask != null) {\n                taskManager.setUncaughtException(e, currentTask.id());\n\n                log.debug(\"Releasing task {} due to uncaught exception.\", currentTask.id());\n                unassignCurrentTask();\n            } else {\n                // If we do not currently have a task assigned and still get an error, this is fatal for the executor thread\n                throw e;\n            }\n        }\n\n        private void runOnce(final long nowMs) {\n            handleTaskReleaseRequested();\n\n            if (currentTask == null) {\n                currentTask = taskManager.assignNextTask(DefaultTaskExecutor.this);\n            }\n\n            if (currentTask == null) {\n                try {\n                    taskManager.awaitProcessableTasks(shutdownRequested::get);\n                } catch (final InterruptedException ignored) {\n                    // Can be ignored, the cause of the interrupted will be handled in the event loop\n                }\n            } else {\n                boolean progressed = false;\n\n                if (taskExecutionMetadata.canProcessTask(currentTask, nowMs) && currentTask.isProcessable(nowMs)) {\n                    if (processTask(currentTask, nowMs, time)) {\n                        log.trace(\"processed a record for {}\", currentTask.id());\n                        progressed = true;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (taskExecutionMetadata.canPunctuateTask(currentTask)) {\n                    if (currentTask.maybePunctuateStreamTime()) {\n                        log.trace(\"punctuated stream time for task {} \", currentTask.id());\n                        progressed = true;\n progressed = true;\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (!progressed) {\n                    log.debug(\"Releasing task {} because we are not making progress.\", currentTask.id());\n                    unassignCurrentTask();\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        private boolean processTask(final Task task, final long now, final Time time) {\n            boolean processed = false;\n            try {\n                processed = task.process(now);\n                if (processed) {\n                    log.trace(\"Successfully processed task (taskExecutionMetadata.hasNamedTopologies() && taskExecutionMetadata.processingMode() != EXACTLY_ONCE_V2) {\n                        taskExecutionMetadata.addToSuccessfullyProcessed(task);\n the following exception; will move to next task and retry later\",\n                        task.id()),\n                    timeoutException\n                );\n            } catch (final TaskMigratedException e) {\n                log.info(\"Failed to process stream task {} since it got migrated to another thread already. \" +\n                    \"Will trigger a new rebalance and close all tasks as zombies together.\", task.id());\n                throw e;\n            } catch (final StreamsException e) {\n                log.error(String.format(\"Failed to process stream task log.error(String.format(\"Failed to process stream task %s due to the following error:\", task.id()), e);\n                throw new StreamsException(e, task.id());\n            } finally {\n                task.recordProcessBatchTime(time.milliseconds() - now);\n            }\n            return processed;\n        }\n\n        private StreamTask unassignCurrentTask() {\n            if (currentTask == null)\n                throw new IllegalStateException(\"Does not own any task while being ask to unassign from task manager\");\n\n            // flush the task before giving it back to task manager, if we are not handing it back because of an error.\n            if (!taskManager.hasUncaughtException(currentTask.id())) {\n                try {\n                    currentTask.flush();\n                } catch (final StreamsException e) {\n                    log.error(String.format(\"Failed to flush stream task %s due to the following error:\", currentTask.id()), e);\n                    e.setTaskId(currentTask.id());\n                    taskManager.setUncaughtException(e, currentTask.id());\n                } catch (final RuntimeException e) {\n                    log.error(String.format(\"Failed to flush stream task %s due to the following error:\", currentTask.id()), e);\n                    taskManager.setUncaughtException(new StreamsException(e, currentTask.id()), currentTask.id());\n                }\n            }\n            taskManager.unassignTask(currentTask, DefaultTaskExecutor.this);\n\n            final StreamTask retTask = currentTask;\n            currentTask = null;\n            return retTask;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private final Time time;\n    private final String name;\n    private final A single instance of this class is\n * shared between all StreamThreads.\n */\npublic class TaskExecutionMetadata {\n    // TODO: implement exponential backoff, for now we just wait 5s\n    private static final long CONSTANT_BACKOFF_MS = 5_000L;\n    private static final long NOT_READY_LOG_INTERVAL_MS = 120_000L; // Log interval of not being ready (2 minutes)\n\n    private final boolean hasNamedTopologies;\n    private final Set<String> pausedTopologies;\n    private final ProcessingMode processingMode;\n    private final Collection<Task> successfullyProcessed = new HashSet<>();\n    // map of topologies experiencing errors/currently under backoff\n    private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, NamedTopologyMetadata> topologyNameToErrorMetadata = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();\n    // map of task to last not ready logging time (not present means ready, >= 0 means not ready and tracks last log time)\n    private final ConcurrentHashMap<TaskId, Long> taskToLastNotReadyLogTime = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();\n    private final Logger log;\n\n    public TaskExecutionMetadata(final Set<String> allTopologyNames,\n                                 final Set<String> pausedTopologies,\n                                 final ProcessingMode processingMode) {\n        this.hasNamedTopologies = !(allTopologyNames.size() == 1 && allTopologyNames.contains(UNNAMED_TOPOLOGY));\n        this.pausedTopologies = pausedTopologies;\n        this.processingMode = processingMode;\n        this.log = new LogContext(\"\").logger(TaskExecutionMetadata.class);\n    }\n\n    public boolean hasNamedTopologies() {\n        return hasNamedTopologies;\n    }\n\n    public ProcessingMode processingMode() {\n        return processingMode;\n    }\n\n    public boolean canProcessTask(final Task task, final long now) {\n        final String topologyName = task.id().topologyName();\n        final boolean taskWasReady = !taskToLastNotReadyLogTime.containsKey(task.id());\n        final boolean canProcess;\n        final String logMessage;\n        \n        if (!hasNamedTopologies) {\n            // TODO implement error handling/backoff for non-named topologies (needs KIP)\n            canProcess = !pausedTopologies.contains(UNNAMED_TOPOLOGY);\n            if (canProcess) {\n                logMessage = String.format(\"Task %s can be processed: topology is not paused\", task.id());\n            } else {\n                logMessage = String.format(\"Task %s can't be processed: topology is paused\", task.id());\n            }\n        } else {\n            if (pausedTopologies.contains(topologyName)) {\n                canProcess = false;\n                logMessage = String.format(\"Task %s can't be processed: topology '%s' is paused\", task.id(), topologyName);\n            } else {\n                final NamedTopologyMetadata metadata = topologyNameToErrorMetadata.get(topologyName);\n                canProcess = metadata == null || (metadata.canProcess() && metadata.canProcessTask(task, now));\n                if (canProcess) {\n                    logMessage = String.format(\"Task %s can be processed for named topology '%s'\", task.id(), topologyName);\n                } else {\n                    logMessage = String.format(\"Task %s can't be processed for named topology '%s'\", task.id(), topologyName);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        \n        if (!canProcess) {\n            if (taskWasReady) {\n                // READY -> NOT_READY - start timer\n                taskToLastNotReadyLogTime.put(task.id(), now);\n            } else {\n                // NOT_READY - check if it should log\n                maybeLogNotReady(task.id(), now, logMessage);\n            }\n        } else {\n            // Task is ready - clear the timer\n            taskToLastNotReadyLogTime.remove(task.id());\n            log.trace(logMessage);\n        }\n        \n        return canProcess;\n    }\n    \n    private void maybeLogNotReady(final TaskId taskId, final long now, final String logMessage) {\n        final Long lastLogTime = taskToLastNotReadyLogTime.get(taskId);\n        if (lastLogTime == null) {\n            return;\n        }\n        \n        final long timeSinceLastLog = now - lastLogTime;\n        if (timeSinceLastLog >= NOT_READY_LOG_INTERVAL_MS) {\n            log.info(\"Task {} is not ready to process: {}\", taskId, logMessage != null ? logMessage : \"Task cannot be processed\");\n            taskToLastNotReadyLogTime.put(taskId, now);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public boolean canPunctuateTask(final Task task) {\n        final String topologyName = task.id().topologyName();\n\n        if (topologyName == null) {\n            return !pausedTopologies.contains(UNNAMED_TOPOLOGY);\n        } else {\n            return !pausedTopologies.contains(topologyName);\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void registerTaskError(final Task task, final Throwable t, final long now) {\n        if (hasNamedTopologies) {\n            final String topologyName = task.id().topologyName();\n            topologyNameToErrorMetadata.computeIfAbsent(topologyName, n -> new NamedTopologyMetadata(topologyName))\n                .registerTaskError(task, t, now);\n        }\n    }\n\n    Collection<Task> successfullyProcessed() {\n        return successfullyProcessed;\n    }\n\n    public void addToSuccessfullyProcessed(final Task task) {\n        successfullyProcessed.add(task);\n    }\n\n    void removeTaskFromSuccessfullyProcessedBeforeClosing(final Task task) {\n        successfullyProcessed.remove(task);\n    }\n\n    void clearSuccessfullyProcessed() {\n        successfullyProcessed.clear();\n    }\n    \n    void removeTaskFromNotReadyTracking(final Task task) {\n        final TaskId taskId = task.id();\n        taskToLastNotReadyLogTime.remove(taskId);\n    }\n\n    private class NamedTopologyMetadata {\n        private final Logger log;\n        private final Map<TaskId, Long> tasksToErrorTime = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();\n\n        public NamedTopologyMetadata(final String topologyName) {\n            final LogContext logContext = new LogContext(String.format(\"topology-name [%s] \", topologyName));\n            this.log = logContext.logger(NamedTopologyMetadata.class);\n        }\n\n        public boolean canProcess() {\n            // TODO: during long task backoffs, pause the full topology to avoid it getting out of sync\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        public boolean canProcessTask(final Task task, final long now) {\n            final Long errorTime = tasksToErrorTime.get(task.id());\n            if (errorTime == null) {\n                return true;\n            } else if (now - errorTime > CONSTANT_BACKOFF_MS) {\n                log.info(\"End backoff for task {} at t={}\", task.id(), now);\n                tasksToErrorTime.remove(task.id());\n                if (tasksToErrorTime.isEmpty()) {\n                    topologyNameToErrorMetadata.remove(task.id().topologyName());\n                }\n                return true;\n            } else {\n                log.debug(\"Skipping processing for unhealthy task {} at t={}\", task.id(), now);\n                return false;\n            }\n        }\n\n        public synchronized void registerTaskError(final Task task, final Throwable t, final long now) {\n            log.info(\"Begin backoff for unhealthy task {} at t={} due to {}\", task.id(), now, t.getClass().getName());\n            tasksToErrorTime.put(task.id(), now);\n        }\n    }\n}\n","numLines":204,"startLine":1,"totalLines":204}}}

pendingActiveTasksToCreate.keySet().removeAll(pendingActiveTasksForTopologies.keySet());\n\n        return pendingActiveTasksForTopologies;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Map<TaskId, filterMap(pendingStandbyTasksToCreate, t -> currentTopologies.contains(t.getKey().topologyName()));\n\n        pendingStandbyTasksToCreate.keySet().removeAll(pendingActiveTasksForTopologies.keySet());\n\n        return pendingActiveTasksForTopologies;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void Set<StreamTask> drainPendingActiveTasksToInit() {\n        final Set<StreamTask> result = new HashSet<>();\n        final Iterator<Task> iterator = pendingTasksToInit.iterator();\n        while    }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Set<StandbyTask> drainPendingStandbyTasksToInit() {\n        final Set<StandbyTask> result = new HashSet<>();\n        final result.add((StandbyTask) task);\n                iterator.remove();\n            }\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Set<Task> pendingTasksToInit() {\n         }\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void addStandbyTasks(final Collection<StandbyTask> newTasks) {\n        if (!newTasks.isEmpty()) {\n            for (final StandbyTask           addActiveTask((StreamTask) task);\n        } else {\n            addStandbyTask((StandbyTask) task);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public synchronized void addActiveTask(final StreamTask task) {\n        final TaskId taskId = task.id();\n\n        if (activeTasksPerId.containsKey(taskId)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempted to create an active task that we already own: \" + taskId);\n        }\n\n        if (standbyTasksPerId.containsKey(taskId)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempted to create an active task while we already own its standby: \" + taskId);\n        }\n\n        activeTasksPerId.put(taskId, task);\n        pendingActiveTasksToCreate.remove(taskId);\n        for (final TopicPartition topicPartition : task.inputPartitions()) {\n            activeTasksPerPartition.put(topicPartition, task);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public synchronized void addStandbyTask(final StandbyTask task) {\n        final TaskId taskId = task.id();\n\n        if (standbyTasksPerId.containsKey(taskId)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempted to create an standby task that we already own: \" + taskId);\n        }\n\n        if (activeTasksPerId.containsKey(taskId)) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempted to create an standby task while we already own its active: \" + taskId);\n        }\n\n        standbyTasksPerId.put(taskId, task);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void addFailedTask(final Task task) {\n        failedTaskIds.add(task.id());\n Task.State.CLOSED && taskToRemove.state() != State.SUSPENDED) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempted to remove a task that is not closed or suspended: \" + taskId);\n        }\n\n        if (pendingTasksToClose.contains(taskToRemove)) {\n            pendingTasksToClose.remove(taskToRemove);\n        } else if (taskToRemove.isActive()) {\n            if (activeTasksPerId.remove(taskId) == null) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Attempted to remove an active task that is not owned: \" + taskId);\n            }\n            removePartitionsForActiveTask(taskId);\n        } else {\n            if (standbyTasksPerId.remove(taskId) == null) {\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Attempted to remove a standby task that is not owned: \" + taskId);\n            }\n        }\n        failedTaskIds.remove(taskId);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public synchronized void replaceStandbyWithActive(final StreamTask activeTask) {\n        final TaskId taskId = activeTask.id();\n        if (standbyTasksPerId.remove(taskId) == null) {\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Attempted to convert unknown standby task to stream task: \" + taskId);\n        }\n\n        activeTasksPerId.put(activeTask.id(), activeTask);\n        for (final TopicPartition topicPartition : activeTask.inputPartitions()) {\n            activeTasksPerPartition.put(topicPartition, activeTask);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean updateActiveTaskInputPartitions(final StreamTask task, final Set<TopicPartition> topicPartitions) {\n        final boolean requiresUpdate = !task.inputPartitions().equals(topicPartitions);\n        if (requiresUpdate) {\n            log.debug(\"Update task {} inputPartitions: current {}, new {}\", task, task.inputPartitions(), topicPartitions);\n            for (final TopicPartition inputPartition : task.inputPartitions()) {\n                activeTasksPerPartition.remove(inputPartition);\n            }\n            for (final TopicPartition topicPartition : topicPartitions) {\n                activeTasksPerPartition.put(topicPartition, task);\n            }\n        }\n\n        return requiresUpdate;\n    }\n\n    private void removePartitionsForActiveTask(final TaskId taskId) {\n        final Set<TopicPartition> toBeRemoved = activeTasksPerPartition.entrySet().stream()\n            .filter(e -> e.getValue().id().equals(taskId))\n            .map(Map.Entry::getKey)\n            .collect(Collectors.toSet());\n        toBeRemoved.forEach(activeTasksPerPartition::remove);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public synchronized void clear() {\n        pendingTasksToInit.clear();\n        pendingTasksToClose.clear();\n        pendingActiveTasksToCreate.clear();\n        pendingStandbyTasksToCreate.clear();\n        activeTasksPerId.clear();\n        standbyTasksPerId.clear();\n        activeTasksPerPartition.clear();\n        failedTaskIds.clear();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public StreamTask activeInitializedTasksForInputPartition(final TopicPartition partition) {\n        return activeTasksPerPartition.get(partition);\n    }\n\n    private synchronized Task getTask(final TaskId taskId) {\n        if (activeTasksPerId.containsKey(taskId)) {\n            return activeTasksPerId.get(taskId);\n        }\n        if (standbyTasksPerId.containsKey(taskId)) {\n            return standbyTasksPerId.get(taskId);\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Task initializedTask(final TaskId taskId) {\n        final Task task = getTask(taskId);\n\n        if (task != null)\n            return task;\n        else\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Task unknown: \" + taskId);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Collection<Task> initializedTasks(final Collection<TaskId> taskIds) {\n        final Set<Task> tasks = new HashSet<>();\n        for (final TaskId taskId : taskIds) {\n            tasks.add(initializedTask(taskId));\n        }\n        return tasks;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public synchronized Collection<TaskId> activeInitializedTaskIds() {\n        return Collections.unmodifiableCollection(activeTasksPerId.keySet());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public synchronized Collection<StreamTask> totalProcessed = 0;\n        Task lastProcessed = null;\n\n        for (final StreamTask task : tasks.activeInitializedTasks()) {\n            final long now = time.milliseconds();\n            try {\n                if (executionMetadata.canProcessTask(task, now)) {\n                    lastProcessed = task;\n                    totalProcessed += processTask(task, maxNumRecords, now, time);\n                }\n            } catch (final Throwable t) {\n                executionMetadata.registerTaskError(task, t, now);\n                executionMetadata.removeTaskFromSuccessfullyProcessedBeforeClosing(lastProcessed);\n                commitSuccessfullyProcessedTasks();\n                throw t;\n            }\n        }\n\n }\n            // TODO: enable regardless of whether using named topologies\n            if (processed > 0 && executionMetadata.hasNamedTopologies() && executionMetadata.processingMode() != EXACTLY_ONCE_V2) {\n                log.trace(\"Successfully processed task {}\", task.id());\n                executionMetadata.addToSuccessfullyProcessed(task);\n            }\n        } catch (final TimeoutException timeoutException) {\n            // TODO consolidate TimeoutException retries with general error handling\n            task.maybeInitTaskTimeoutOrThrow(now, timeoutException);\n            log.error(\n                String.format(\n                    \"Could not complete processing records for %s due to the following exception; will move to next task and retry later\",\n                    task.id()),\n                timeoutException\n            );\n        } catch (final TaskMigratedException e) {\n            log.info(\"Failed to process stream task {} since it got migrated to another thread already. \" +\n                \"Will trigger a new rebalance and close all tasks as zombies together.\", task.id());\n            throw e;\n new StreamsException(e, task.id());\n        } finally {\n            now = time.milliseconds();\n            task.recordProcessBatchTime(now - then);\n        }\n        return processed;\n    }\n\n Since `tasksLock` is a ReentrantLock, this nested acquisition should work fine.\n\nThe key thing is that the inner `returnWithTasksLocked()` increments the hold count, runs its lambda, then decrements it back down. The lock stays held until the outer `returnWithTasksLocked()` finally releases it. The callback is triggered from `handleTaskReleaseRequested()`, which is called early in `runOnce()` before any locks are acquired. The `unassignCurrentTask()` call acquires and releases `tasksLock` internally, so by the time we reach `taskReleaseFuture.complete()`, the lock is already released. This means the callback runs without `tasksLock` held, so there's no deadlock from that particular path.\n\nBut there's another potential issue: what if a callback registered on `lockTasks` tries to call `result.complete()` itself, which would then trigger downstream callbacks?\n\nLooking at `maybeLockTasks()`, it just calls `.get()` on the future without registering any callbacks, so that's not a concern. And `lockAllTasks()` isn't even used directly in the codebase. I think I'm overcomplicating this—let me step back and look at the actual test patterns to understand how the DefaultTaskManager is supposed to
